Apples to Apples

Apples To Apples: A fun party game for the whole mush or family. It includes every unique card made for the Apples To Apples game (Over 1700 red cards and 500 green cards!).

Author: Walker@M*U*S*H
Category: Games
Commands: @assert, @break, @dolist, @emit, @name, @oemit, @parent, @pemit, @set, @teleport, @wait, @wipe.
Functions: after(), align(), ansi(), before(), cat(), cor(), create(), decompose(), default(), edit(), eq(), extract(), filterbool(), first(), firstof(), get(), grep(), gt(), gte(), hasattr(), hasattrval(), idle(), if(), inc(), itemize(), iter(), last(), lattr(), lattrp(), lflags(), loc(), lwho(), map(), match(), member(), mul(), name(), not(), poss(), randword(), regeditall(), setdiff(), setq(), setr(), setunion(), shuffle(), sortkey(), space(), squish(), strcat(), strmatch(), sub(), switch(), u(), v(), width(), words().
Features: #lambda.
Compatibility: CobraMUSH, PennMUSH.

Instructions

Copy and paste the below code into a compatible MUSH or MUX.

MUSHCode for Apples to Apples

Select Code
@@ Project walkerApplesToApples
@@ Version 9
@@
@@ Description:
@@ Apples To Apples: A fun party game for the whole mush or
@@ family. It includes every unique card made for the Apples To
@@ Apples game (Over 1700 red cards and 500 green cards!). You
@@ can add your own cards by using R` and G` attributes!
@@
@@ Version log:
@@ Author: Walker <Mush>
@@ Date: Thu Dec 11 15:30:28 2008 -0800
@@ v9v
@@
@@ Added s`notyourturn
@@
@@ Readme:
@@ You can add your own cards by using R`... and G`...
@@ attributes on the Apples To Apples object. Please don't
@@ touch the "Official" card decks.
@@
@@ Language: MushCode
@@ Installer file created by RubySVC (Softcode Version Control)
@@
@@
@@
@@ Creating Rooms, Things and Exits.
@@
@@
@set me=SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0:[default(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0,create(T4f87846659f79afb94f0))]
@set me=SVC`T246fbce3c4a4f44cb726:[default(SVC`T246fbce3c4a4f44cb726,create(T246fbce3c4a4f44cb726))]
@set me=SVC`Te6a5d06fe9f72be178bf:[default(SVC`Te6a5d06fe9f72be178bf,create(Te6a5d06fe9f72be178bf))]
@@
@@
@@ Objects created, now setting attributes, locks, etc.
@@
@@
@@
@@ Filling out Apples To Apples
@@
@parent [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=v(SVC`T246fbce3c4a4f44cb726)
@name [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=Apples To Apples
@lock/BASIC [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]==%!
@set [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=iter(setdiff(lflags([v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]),OPAQUE VISUAL),!##) [setdiff(OPAQUE VISUAL,lflags([v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]))]
@set [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=VR:[v(SVC`Te6a5d06fe9f72be178bf)]
@set [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=VG:[v(SVC`T246fbce3c4a4f44cb726)]
&USE [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=[ansi(r,Apples)] To [ansi(g,Apples)] Commands:%r%r[ansi(h,about apples)] - Get an overview of just what Apples To Apples is.%r%r[ansi(h,join apples)] - Join the game!%r[ansi(h,quit apples)] - Toss your cards and leave.%r[ansi(h,clear apples)] - reset the game.%r[ansi(h,draw green)] - Draw a green card if you're the winner or starting a game.%r[space(12)] (You can also draw green if the winner is over 10 minutes idle)%r[ansi(h,hand)] - See your red cards.%r[ansi(h,play <cardname>)] - Play a red card from your hand. (Judges, not for you!)%r[ansi(h,read cards)] - Read all the currently submitted red cards.%r[ansi(h,choose <cardname>)] - Judge: Choose the winning card!%r[ansi(h,green apples)] - Find out how many green apples players have!
&S`WRONGTIME [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=Wrong time to do that.
&S`WINNERCHOSEN [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=%n selects "[u(fun`cardname,%0)]" as the winner!
&S`WINNER [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=[name(%0)] played the winning card, and [switch(%1,1,gets [poss(%0)] first green card!,gets the card for a total of %1 points!)] [name(%0)], it is now your turn. Use "[ansi(h,draw green)]" to start the next round!
&S`WHICHONE [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=Which one?
&S`SCORE`LINE [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=first(align(>12 >3 <10,name(last(%0,`)),ansi(g,v(%0)),ansi(g,apples)),%r)
&S`SCORE [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=Score:%r%r[map(s`score`line,sortkey(#lambda/v(\%0),lattr(me/play`score`#*)),%b,%r)]
&S`READS [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=%n turns over the [words(lattr(me/play`round`#*))] red cards one by one and slowly reads them out, looking for a best fit for: "[u(fun`greenname,v(play`round`green))]"
&S`QUIT [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=You quit the game. :-(. Come back soon!
&S`OQUIT [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=%n quits the game.
&S`OJOINED [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=%n joins the game.
&S`OCLEARGAME [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=%n clears the Apples to Apples game.
&S`OCHOOSERED [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=%n plucks out a Red Apple card and tosses it onto the pile.
&S`NOTYOURTURN [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=It's not your turn to draw a green card!
&S`NOTJUDGE [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=You aren't the judge!
&S`NOTJOINED [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=You aren't playing!
&S`NOTENOUGH [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=You need at least 2 red cards to choose between!
&S`NEWTURN [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=%n draws a green card and reads it out loud: "[u(fun`greenfull,%0)]"
&S`NEWCARD [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=You draw a new red card: "[u(fun`cardname,%0)]"
&S`JOINED [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=You join the game, drawing 7 red apple cards.
&S`HANDPLAY [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=Use [ansi(h,hand)] to see your hand, and [ansi(h,play <cardname>)] to play your card!
&S`CLEARGAME [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=You clear the Apples to Apples game.
&S`CHOOSEWINNER [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=Use "[ansi(h,choose <card>)]" to choose the winner!
&S`CHOOSERED [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=You pluck out "[u(fun`cardname,%0)]" and toss it onto the pile.
&S`ALREADYPLAYED [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=You've already played a card!
&S`ALREADYJOINED [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=You've already joined!
&S`ALLCHOSE [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=All players have chosen cards. [name(v(play`round`judge))], you might want to "[ansi(h,read cards)]"
&S`ABOUT [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=About%r%rApples To Apples is a family party game intended for 3 or more players. (Typically 10 at max, but there's no reason not to have more!). %r%rThere are two types of cards, or "apples" here: Green apples, which are adjectives, and Red Apples, which can be people, events, places, objects, etcetera.%r%rThe object of the game is to pick your red card that best matches the judge's green card. A game consists of many rounds: Each round has two stages: The choosing stage, and the judging stage.%r%rA round starts when a green card is drawn by the judge, and is read out loud to the players. All players (except the judge!) must then play a red card from their hand that they feel would either best match the card in any way: Literally, ironically, laughably, etc. Don't worry - be silly. For "cuddly", you can get a lot of laughs for playing "Cactus"!.%r%rWhen the playing round is over (you need at least 2 cards to judge!), the judge will read the cards aloud, one by one, and pick the one that they think best fits with the green card they drew. They must give a reason. There's no point to a party game if you can't argue and chat about your decision!%r%rWhen the judge chooses a winner, that player gets the green card as a point, and is then the next to judge!%r%rWinning: Typically, a group will play until it gets tired of Apples To Apples, and name the one with the most green cards as winner.
&SVC`IGNORE [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=play`* r`* g`*
&SVC [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=SVC configuration
&S [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=Messages.
&REPLY [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=[ansi(r,Apples)] to [ansi(g,Apples)]: [firstof(u(%0,%1,%2,%3,%4),%0)]
&R [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]="Local" red cards.
&PLAY [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=Play tree for the current game.
&G [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]="Local" green cards.
&FUN`RED [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=switch(%0,R`*,v(%0),get(%vr/%0))
&FUN`PICKCARD [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=filterbool(#lambda/cor(strmatch(before(setr(x,u(fun`red,\%0)),|),[decompose(%1)]*),strmatch(before(\%qx,|),*%b[decompose(%1)]*)),%0)
&FUN`HAND [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=Your hand:%r[map(#lambda/u(fun`desccard,\%0,r),v(play`%#),%b,%r)]
&FUN`GREENNAME [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=ansi(g,squish(before(u(fun`green,%0),|)))
&FUN`GREENFULL [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=ansi(g,squish(before(setr(x,u(fun`green,%0)),|))) - [squish(after(%qx,|))]
&FUN`GREENCARD [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=align(>20 <[sub(width(%#),25)],ansi(g,squish(before(setr(x,u(fun`green,%0)),|))),squish(after(%qx,|)))
&FUN`GREEN [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=switch(%0,G`*,v(%0),get(%vg/%0))
&FUN`DRAWRED [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=extract(shuffle(setdiff(lattrp(me/r`*) [lattr(%vr)],cat(v(play`red),iter(lattr(me/play`#*),v(##))))),1,%0)
&FUN`DESCGREEN [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=align(>20 <[sub(width(%#),25)],ansi(g,squish(before(setr(x,u(fun`green,%0)),|))),squish(after(%qx,|)))
&FUN`DESCCARD [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=align(>20 <[sub(width(%#),25)],ansi(r,squish(before(setr(x,u(fun`red,%0)),|))),squish(after(%qx,|)))
&FUN`CARDNAME [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=ansi(r,squish(before(u(fun`red,%0),|)))
&FUN`CARDFULL [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=ansi(r,squish(before(setr(x,u(fun`red,%0)),|))) - [squish(after(%qx,|))]
&FUN [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=Functions.
&DESCRIBE`SCORED [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=strcat(The green card was:%r,u(fun`desccard,v(play`round`green),g),%r%rThe winning card was:%b,u(fun`cardname,v(play`round`[v(play`lastwinner)])),\, played by%b,name(v(play`lastwinner))!,%r%rThe red cards were:%r[map(#lambda/u(fun`desccard,\%0,r),shuffle(iter(lattr(me/play`round`#*),v(##))),%b,%r)],%r%r,name(v(play`lastwinner)) - Type "[ansi(h,draw green)]" to get the next round started!)
&DESCRIBE`JUDGING [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=strcat(The current judge is:%b,name(v(play`round`judge)).%r%rThe current green card is:%r,u(fun`greencard,v(play`round`green),g),%r%rThe red cards are:%r[map(#lambda/u(fun`desccard,\%0,r),shuffle(iter(lattr(me/play`round`#*),v(##))),%b,%r)]%r%rJudge\, type [ansi(h,choose <cardname>)] to pick a winner!
&DESCRIBE`CLEARED [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=The game has not yet started. Use "[ansi(h,draw green)]" to start a round!
&DESCRIBE`CHOOSING [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=strcat(The current judge is:%b,name(v(play`round`judge)).%r%rThe current green card is:%r,u(fun`descgreen,v(play`round`green),g),%r%r[if(setr(r,setdiff(edit(lattr(me/PLAY`#*),PLAY`,),cat(v(play`round`judge),edit(lattr(me/play`round`#*),PLAY`ROUND`,)))),regeditall(itemize(%qr),#\\d+,name($0)) [if(gt(words(%qr),1),have,has)] not tossed in red cards.,Everybody has tossed in their red cards.)]%r%r[if(member(v(play`round`judge),%#),%n - Type "[ansi(h,read cards)]" to start the judging!,if(hasattr(me,play`round`%#),You played: [u(fun`cardname,v(play`round`%#))],%n - Type "[ansi(h,hand)]" to see your hand\, and "[ansi(h,play <cardname>)]" to play your card!))]
&DESCRIBE [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=[ansi(r,Apples)] to [ansi(g,Apples)] game.%r%rCurrently holding cards: [firstof(regeditall(itemize(edit(lattr(me/play`#*),PLAY`,)),#\\d+,name($0)),nobody)]%r%r[firstof(u(describe`[firstof(v(play`round),cleared)]),Game state: [v(play`round)])][if(not(hasattr(me,play`%#)),%r%rType [ansi(h,use [name(me)])] for help!)]
&CMD`SCORING [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=$green apples:@pemit %#=u(reply,s`score)
&CMD`READCARDS [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=$read cards:@assert hasattr(me,play`%#)=@pemit %#=u(reply,s`notjoined) ; @assert member(v(play`round),choosing)=@pemit %#=u(reply,s`wrongtime) ; @assert member(v(play`round`judge),%#)=@pemit %#=u(reply,s`notjudge) ; @assert gte(words(lattr(me/play`round`#*)),2)=@pemit %#=u(reply,s`notenough) ; @emit u(reply,s`reads) ; &play`round me=judging ; @dolist shuffle(lattr(me/play`round`#*))=@wait mul(#@,3)=@emit %n says, "[u(fun`cardfull,v(##))]" ; @wait mul(inc(words(lattr(me/play`round`#*))),3)=@pemit %#=u(reply,s`choosewinner)
&CMD`QUIT [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=$quit apples:@assert hasattr(me,play`%#)=@pemit %#=u(reply,s`notjoined) ; @wipe me/play`%# ; @pemit %#=u(reply,s`quit) ; @oemit loc(me)/%#=u(reply,s`oquit)
&CMD`PLAY [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=$play *:@assert hasattrval(me,play`%#)=@pemit %#=u(reply,s`notjoined) ; @assert member(choosing,v(play`round))=@pemit %#=u(reply,s`wrongtime) ; @break match(v(play`round`judge),%#)=@pemit %#=u(reply,s`nojudge) ; @break hasattrval(me,play`round`%#)=@pemit %#=u(reply,s`alreadyplayed) ; @assert eq(words(setr(0,u(fun`pickcard,v(play`%#),%0))),1)=@pemit %#=u(reply,s`whichone,%q0) ; @pemit %#=u(reply,s`choosered,%q0) ; @oemit loc(me)/%#=u(reply,s`ochoosered) ; &play`round`%# me=%q0 ; &play`%# me=setunion(setdiff(v(play`%#),%q0),setr(r,u(fun`drawred,1))) ; &play`red me=extract(%q0 [v(play`red)],1,200) ; @pemit %#=u(reply,s`newcard,%qr) ; @assert eq(inc(words(lattr(me/play`round`#*))),words(lattr(me/play`#*))) ; @emit u(reply,s`allchose)
&CMD`JOIN [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=$join apples:@break hasattr(me,play`%#)=@pemit %#=u(reply,s`alreadyjoined) ; &play`%# me=u(fun`drawred,7) ; @pemit %#=u(reply,s`joined) ; @oemit loc(me)/%#=u(reply,s`ojoined) ; @pemit %#=u(fun`hand,%#)
&CMD`HAND [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=$hand:@assert hasattrval(me,play`%#)=@pemit %#=u(reply,s`notjoined) ; @pemit %#=u(reply,u(fun`hand,%0))
&CMD`DRAWGREEN [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=$draw green:@assert hasattrval(me,play`%#)=@pemit %#=u(reply,s`notjoined) ; @break member(choosing judging,v(play`round))=@pemit %#=u(reply,s`wrongtime) ; @assert cor(not(v(play`lastwinner)),member(v(play`lastwinner),%#),gte(idle(v(play`lastwinner)),300),not(member(lwho(),v(play`lastwinner))))=@pemit %#=u(reply,s`notyourturn) ; @wipe me/play`round`** ; &play`round me=choosing ; &play`round`judge me=%# ; &play`round`green me=setr(g,randword(setdiff(lattrp(me/g`*) [lattr(%vg)],v(play`green)))) ; &play`green me=extract(%qg [v(play`green)],1,40) ; @emit u(reply,s`newturn,%qg) ; @oemit loc(%!)/%#=u(reply,s`handplay)
&CMD`CLEAR [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=$clear apples:@oemit loc(me)/%#=u(reply,s`ocleargame) ; @pemit %#=u(reply,s`cleargame) ; @wipe me/play`** ; &play`red me ; &play`green me
&CMD`CHOOSE [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=$choose *:@assert hasattrval(me,play`%#)=@pemit %#=u(reply,s`notjoined) ; @assert member(judging,v(play`round))=@pemit %#=u(reply,s`wrongtime) ; @assert member(%#,v(play`round`judge))=@pemit %#=u(reply,s`notjudge) ; @assert eq(words(setr(0,u(fun`pickcard,iter(lattr(me/play`round`#*),v(##)),%0))),1)=@pemit %#=u(reply,s`whichone,%q0) ; @emit u(reply,s`winnerchosen,%q0) ; think setq(w,edit(grep(me,play`round`#*,%q0),PLAY`ROUND`,)) ; &play`round me=scored ; &play`lastwinner me=%qw ; &play`score`%qw me=firstof(inc(v(play`score`%qw)),1) ; @wait 1=@emit u(reply,s`winner,%qw,v(play`score`%qw))
&CMD`ABOUT [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=$about apples:@pemit %#=u(reply,s`about)
&CMD [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]=Commands.
@set [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]/USE=no_command prefixmatch
@set [v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]/DESCRIBE=no_command visual prefixmatch public nearby
@@
@@ Filling out Official Green Apple Cards
@@
@name [v(SVC`T246fbce3c4a4f44cb726)]=Official Green Apple Cards
@lock/BASIC [v(SVC`T246fbce3c4a4f44cb726)]==[v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)]
@tel [v(SVC`T246fbce3c4a4f44cb726)]=v(SVC`T4f87846659f79afb94f0)
@set [v(SVC`T246fbce3c4a4f44cb726)]=iter(setdiff(lflags([v(SVC`T246fbce3c4a4f44cb726)]),NO_COMMAND VISUAL),!##) [setdiff(NO_COMMAND VISUAL,lflags([v(SVC`T246fbce3c4a4f44cb726)]))]
&Z [v(SVC`T246fbce3c4a4f44cb726)]=Confused|(muddled, bewildered, perplexed)
&Y [v(SVC`T246fbce3c4a4f44cb726)]=Complicated|(difficult, complex, involved)
&X [v(SVC`T246fbce3c4a4f44cb726)]=Comical|(funny, hilarious, amusing)
&W [v(SVC`T246fbce3c4a4f44cb726)]=Comfortable|(cozy, snug, restful)
&V [v(SVC`T246fbce3c4a4f44cb726)]=Colorful|(vivid, brilliant, kaleidoscopic)
&U [v(SVC`T246fbce3c4a4f44cb726)]=Cold|(chilly, icy, aloof)
&T [v(SVC`T246fbce3c4a4f44cb726)]=Clueless|(unaware, oblivious, ignorant)
&S [v(SVC`T246fbce3c4a4f44cb726)]=Clean|(washed, pure, tidy)
&R [v(SVC`T246fbce3c4a4f44cb726)]=Classic|(timeless, definitive, vintage)
&Q [v(SVC`T246fbce3c4a4f44cb726)]=Chunky|(lumpy, chubby, bumpy)
&P [v(SVC`T246fbce3c4a4f44cb726)]=Chewy|(gummy, rubbery, stringy)
&O [v(SVC`T246fbce3c4a4f44cb726)]=Cheesy|(trashy, tawdry, far-fetched)
&N [v(SVC`T246fbce3c4a4f44cb726)]=Charming|(captivating, enchanting, fascinating)
&M [v(SVC`T246fbce3c4a4f44cb726)]=Charismatic|(alluring, magnetic, charming)
&L [v(SVC`T246fbce3c4a4f44cb726)]=Casual|(easygoing, blase, nonchalant)
&K [v(SVC`T246fbce3c4a4f44cb726)]=Calm|(peaceful, tranquil, placid)
&J [v(SVC`T246fbce3c4a4f44cb726)]=Busy|(occupied, meddlesome, engrossed)
&I [v(SVC`T246fbce3c4a4f44cb726)]=Brilliant|(dazzling, gleaming, intelligent)
&H [v(SVC`T246fbce3c4a4f44cb726)]=Bright|(brilliant, radiant, shiny)
&G [v(SVC`T246fbce3c4a4f44cb726)]=Boring|(dull, tedious, monotonous)
&F [v(SVC`T246fbce3c4a4f44cb726)]=Bold|(daring, brave, courageous)
&E0 [v(SVC`T246fbce3c4a4f44cb726)]=Yucky|(icky, sickening)
